.1.96+ puede mandar una etiqueta explícita; la usamos sólo si no contradice el raw operativo.
  if(explicit)return explicit;

  // No tocar comportamiento FULL/FLEX: Full queda como bodega; Flex conserva su lógica propia.
  if(logistic==='FULL'&&(blob.includes('ready_to_ship')||blob.includes('pending')||blob.includes('handling')||blob.includes('packed')))return 'Procesando en bodega';

  // Si fue refrescado desde ML y es Mercado Envíos común, evitamos falso rojo por status base ready_to_ship.
  // ML suele conservar ready_to_ship mientras el subestado/seguimiento real avanza.
  if(ch==='ML'&&logistic==='Mercado Envíos'&&refreshed&&blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'En camino';

  if(blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'Listo para despachar';
  if(blob.includes('not_shipped')||blob.includes('unpacked')||blob.includes('unfulfilled'))return 'Sin despachar';
  if(blob.includes('pending'))return 'Pendiente';
  if(opt)return opt;
  return '';
}
function shippingStateClass(label){
  let raw=String(label||'').toLowerCase();
  if(raw.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered'))return 'delivered';
  if(raw.includes('a coordinar'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('pendiente'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('despacharemos'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('procesando'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('listo')||raw.includes('despachar')||raw.includes('sin despachar'))return 'pending';
  return 'other';
}
function invoiceOrderId(o,ch){
  if(ch==='ML'){
    let ids=Array.isArray(o.child_order_ids)?o.child_order_ids.filter(Boolean):[];
    if(ids.length)return ids[0];
  }
  return o.external_order_id||o.id||'';
}
function invoiceButton(o,ch){
  // Sólo ventas entregadas y todavía no facturadas muestran la acción.
  // Sin icono significa: ya facturada o todavía no corresponde facturar.
  let st=String(o.invoice_status||o.arca_status||'').toLowerCase();
  let hasCae=!!(o.invoice_cae||o.cae||o.arca_cae);
  if(hasCae||st==='issued')return '';
  let delivered=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').trim().toLowerCase()==='entregado';
  if(!delivered)return '';
  let oid=invoiceOrderId(o,ch);
  if(!oid)return '';
  return `<div class="invoiceMiniWrap"><details class="kebabMenu invoiceKebab"><summary class="invoiceStatusIcon draft" title="Pendiente de facturación">📄⚠️</summary><div class="kebabPanel"><button onclick="issueInvoiceFromSale('${jsq(ch)}','${jsq(oid)}')">Facturar</button></div></details></div>`;
}
function isTnMotoShipping(o){
  let opt=String(o.shipping_option||o.tn_shipping_option||'').toLowerCase();
  return opt.includes('moto')||opt.includes('motomensaj')||opt.includes('mensajería')||opt.includes('mensajeria');
}
function canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch){
  if(ch!=='TN')return false;
  if(!isTnMotoShipping(o))return false;
  let st=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').toLowerCase();
  let raw=shippingStatusText(o);
  let already=!!(o.tn_manual_delivered||o.manual_delivered)||st.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered')||raw.includes('manual_delivered');
  if(already)return false;
  return st.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('shipped');
}
function tnDeliveredButton(o,ch){
  if(!canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch))return '';
  let oid=String(o.external_order_id||'');
  if(!oid)return '';
  let label=String(orderNumber(o,ch)||oid).replace(/'/g,'');
  return `<br><button class="secondary smallBtn" onclick="markTnMotoDelivered('${esc(oid)}','${esc(label)}')">Entregado</button>`;
}
async function markTnMotoDelivered(orderId,label){
  if(!confirm(`Marcar ${label||orderId} como ENTREGADO?\n\nPrimero intento reflejarlo en Tienda Nube. Si TN lo rechaza, igual queda cerrado en el ERP y se guarda el error.`))return;
  setBusy(true,'Marcando entregado','Intentando marcar entregado en Tienda Nube y cerrando ERP...');
  setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Marcando entregado...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/tn/orders/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/mark_delivered_manual?sync_tn=true`,{method:'POST'});
    let tnMsg=d.tn_api_ok?'ERP cerrado; TN respondió OK pero para moto puede quedar shipped':'ERP cerrado; TN no aceptó delivered (ver raw/debug)';
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus',`OK: ${label||orderId} marcado Entregado · ${tnMsg}`,true);
    await loadRecent('TN',state.sales.TN.offset||0);
    loadDashboard(true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Error marcando entregado: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('markTnMotoDelivered',e);
  }finally{setBusy(false)}
}

function orderCard(o,ch){
  let lines=linesForOrder(o);
  let display=lines.map(l=>`<div class="lineItem"><div><strong>${esc(l.sku)}</strong></div><div>${esc(l.name||'')}</div><div>Cant: <strong>${esc(l.quantity)}</strong></div><div>${l.unit_price!==''?money(l.unit_price):''}</div><div>${l.prev!==undefined?`Stock ${esc(l.prev)} → ${esc(l.next)}`:(l.subtotal?money(l.subtotal):'')}</div></div>`).join('')||'<div class="muted">Sin líneas visibles todavía.</div>';
  let sub=subOrderText(o,ch);
  let logistic=logisticLabel(o,ch);
  let logState=shippingStateLabel(o,ch);
  let act=saleNeedsAction(o,ch);
  let stateCls=shippingStateClass(logState);
  let stateHtml=logState?`<span class="shippingAction ${stateCls}">${esc(logState)}</span>`:'';
  let manualDeliveredHtml=tnDeliveredButton(o,ch);
  let showAction=!!(act&&String(act).trim().toLowerCase()!==String(logState||'').trim().toLowerCase());
  let actionHtml=showAction?`<span class="logisticsAction">${esc(act)}</span>`:'';
  let totalSub=o.total_products&&Number(o.total_products)!==Number(o.total)?`<br><span class="small">Productos: ${money(o.total_products)}</span>`:'';
  let logisticClass=logistic==='FULL'?'ship-full':logistic==='FLEX'?'ship-flex':(logistic==='A coordinar'||logistic==='Sin envío')?'ship-coord':'ship-ml';

 la usamos sólo si no contradice el raw operativo.
  if(explicit)return explicit;

  // No tocar comportamiento FULL/FLEX: Full queda como bodega; Flex conserva su lógica propia.
  if(logistic==='FULL'&&(blob.includes('ready_to_ship')||blob.includes('pending')||blob.includes('handling')||blob.includes('packed')))return 'Procesando en bodega';

  // Si fue refrescado desde ML y es Mercado Envíos común, evitamos falso rojo por status base ready_to_ship.
  // ML suele conservar ready_to_ship mientras el subestado/seguimiento real avanza.
  if(ch==='ML'&&logistic==='Mercado Envíos'&&refreshed&&blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'En camino';

  if(blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'Listo para despachar';
  if(blob.includes('not_shipped')||blob.includes('unpacked')||blob.includes('unfulfilled'))return 'Sin despachar';
  if(blob.includes('pending'))return 'Pendiente';
  if(opt)return opt;
  return '';
}
function shippingStateClass(label){
  let raw=String(label||'').toLowerCase();
  if(raw.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered'))return 'delivered';
  if(raw.includes('a coordinar'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('pendiente'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('despacharemos'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('procesando'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('listo')||raw.includes('despachar')||raw.includes('sin despachar'))return 'pending';
  return 'other';
}
function invoiceOrderId(o,ch){
  if(ch==='ML'){
    let ids=Array.isArray(o.child_order_ids)?o.child_order_ids.filter(Boolean):[];
    if(ids.length)return ids[0];
  }
  return o.external_order_id||o.id||'';
}
function invoiceButton(o,ch){
  // Sólo ventas entregadas y todavía no facturadas muestran la acción.
  // Sin icono significa: ya facturada o todavía no corresponde facturar.
  let st=String(o.invoice_status||o.arca_status||'').toLowerCase();
  let hasCae=!!(o.invoice_cae||o.cae||o.arca_cae);
  if(hasCae||st==='issued')return '';
  let delivered=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').trim().toLowerCase()==='entregado';
  if(!delivered)return '';
  let oid=invoiceOrderId(o,ch);
  if(!oid)return '';
  return `<div class="invoiceMiniWrap"><details class="kebabMenu invoiceKebab"><summary class="invoiceStatusIcon draft" title="Pendiente de facturación">📄⚠️</summary><div class="kebabPanel"><button onclick="issueInvoiceFromSale('${jsq(ch)}','${jsq(oid)}')">Facturar</button></div></details></div>`;
}
function isTnMotoShipping(o){
  let opt=String(o.shipping_option||o.tn_shipping_option||'').toLowerCase();
  return opt.includes('moto')||opt.includes('motomensaj')||opt.includes('mensajería')||opt.includes('mensajeria');
}
function canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch){
  if(ch!=='TN')return false;
  if(!isTnMotoShipping(o))return false;
  let st=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').toLowerCase();
  let raw=shippingStatusText(o);
  let already=!!(o.tn_manual_delivered||o.manual_delivered)||st.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered')||raw.includes('manual_delivered');
  if(already)return false;
  return st.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('shipped');
}
function tnDeliveredButton(o,ch){
  if(!canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch))return '';
  let oid=String(o.external_order_id||'');
  if(!oid)return '';
  let label=String(orderNumber(o,ch)||oid).replace(/'/g,'');
  return `<br><button class="secondary smallBtn" onclick="markTnMotoDelivered('${esc(oid)}','${esc(label)}')">Entregado</button>`;
}
async function markTnMotoDelivered(orderId,label){
  if(!confirm(`Marcar ${label||orderId} como ENTREGADO?\n\nPrimero intento reflejarlo en Tienda Nube. Si TN lo rechaza, igual queda cerrado en el ERP y se guarda el error.`))return;
  setBusy(true,'Marcando entregado','Intentando marcar entregado en Tienda Nube y cerrando ERP...');
  setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Marcando entregado...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/tn/orders/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/mark_delivered_manual?sync_tn=true`,{method:'POST'});
    let tnMsg=d.tn_api_ok?'ERP cerrado; TN respondió OK pero para moto puede quedar shipped':'ERP cerrado; TN no aceptó delivered (ver raw/debug)';
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus',`OK: ${label||orderId} marcado Entregado · ${tnMsg}`,true);
    await loadRecent('TN',state.sales.TN.offset||0);
    loadDashboard(true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Error marcando entregado: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('markTnMotoDelivered',e);
  }finally{setBusy(false)}
}

.floatingKebabPanel{posi

explícita; la usamos sólo si no contradice el raw operativo.
  if(explicit)return explicit;

  // No tocar comportamiento FULL/FLEX: Full queda como bodega; Flex conserva su lógica propia.
  if(logistic==='FULL'&&(blob.includes('ready_to_ship')||blob.includes('pending')||blob.includes('handling')||blob.includes('packed')))return 'Procesando en bodega';

  // Si fue refrescado desde ML y es Mercado Envíos común, evitamos falso rojo por status base ready_to_ship.
  // ML suele conservar ready_to_ship mientras el subestado/seguimiento real avanza.
  if(ch==='ML'&&logistic==='Mercado Envíos'&&refreshed&&blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'En camino';

  if(blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'Listo para despachar';
  if(blob.includes('not_shipped')||blob.includes('unpacked')||blob.includes('unfulfilled'))return 'Sin despachar';
  if(blob.includes('pending'))return 'Pendiente';
  if(opt)return opt;
  return '';
}
function shippingStateClass(label){
  let raw=String(label||'').toLowerCase();
  if(raw.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered'))return 'delivered';
  if(raw.includes('a coordinar'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('pendiente'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('despacharemos'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('procesando'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('listo')||raw.includes('despachar')||raw.includes('sin despachar'))return 'pending';
  return 'other';
}
function invoiceOrderId(o,ch){
  if(ch==='ML'){
    let ids=Array.isArray(o.child_order_ids)?o.child_order_ids.filter(Boolean):[];
    if(ids.length)return ids[0];
  }
  return o.external_order_id||o.id||'';
}
function invoiceButton(o,ch){
  // Sólo ventas entregadas y todavía no facturadas muestran la acción.
  // Sin icono significa: ya facturada o todavía no corresponde facturar.
  let st=String(o.invoice_status||o.arca_status||'').toLowerCase();
  let hasCae=!!(o.invoice_cae||o.cae||o.arca_cae);
  if(hasCae||st==='issued')return '';
  let delivered=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').trim().toLowerCase()==='entregado';
  if(!delivered)return '';
  let oid=invoiceOrderId(o,ch);
  if(!oid)return '';
  return `<div class="invoiceMiniWrap"><details class="kebabMenu invoiceKebab"><summary class="invoiceStatusIcon draft" title="Pendiente de facturación">📄⚠️</summary><div class="kebabPanel"><button onclick="issueInvoiceFromSale('${jsq(ch)}','${jsq(oid)}')">Facturar</button></div></details></div>`;
}
function isTnMotoShipping(o){
  let opt=String(o.shipping_option||o.tn_shipping_option||'').toLowerCase();
  return opt.includes('moto')||opt.includes('motomensaj')||opt.includes('mensajería')||opt.includes('mensajeria');
}
function canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch){
  if(ch!=='TN')return false;
  if(!isTnMotoShipping(o))return false;
  let st=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').toLowerCase();
  let raw=shippingStatusText(o);
  let already=!!(o.tn_manual_delivered||o.manual_delivered)||st.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered')||raw.includes('manual_delivered');
  if(already)return false;
  return st.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('shipped');
}
function tnDeliveredButton(o,ch){
  if(!canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch))return '';
  let oid=String(o.external_order_id||'');
  if(!oid)return '';
  let label=String(orderNumber(o,ch)||oid).replace(/'/g,'');
  return `<br><button class="secondary smallBtn" onclick="markTnMotoDelivered('${esc(oid)}','${esc(label)}')">Entregado</button>`;
}
async function markTnMotoDelivered(orderId,label){
  if(!confirm(`Marcar ${label||orderId} como ENTREGADO?\n\nPrimero intento reflejarlo en Tienda Nube. Si TN lo rechaza, igual queda cerrado en el ERP y se guarda el error.`))return;
  setBusy(true,'Marcando entregado','Intentando marcar entregado en Tienda Nube y cerrando ERP...');
  setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Marcando entregado...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/tn/orders/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/mark_delivered_manual?sync_tn=true`,{method:'POST'});
    let tnMsg=d.tn_api_ok?'ERP cerrado; TN respondió OK pero para moto puede quedar shipped':'ERP cerrado; TN no aceptó delivered (ver raw/debug)';
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus',`OK: ${label||orderId} marcado Entregado · ${tnMsg}`,true);
    await loadRecent('TN',state.sales.TN.offset||0);
    loadDashboard(true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Error marcando entregado: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('markTnMotoDelivered',e);
  }finally{setBusy(false)}
}

  let logState=shippingStateLabel(o,ch);

  let stateCls=shippingStateClass(logState);
  let stateHtml=logState?`<span class="shippingAction ${stateCls}">${esc(logState)}</span>`:'';
  let manualDeliveredHtml=tnDeliveredButton(o,ch);
  let showAction=!!(act&&String(act).trim().toLowerCase()!==String(logState||'').trim().toLowerCase());
  let actionHtml=showAction?`<span class="logisticsAction">${esc(act)}</span>`:'';
  let totalSub=o.total_products&&Number(o.total_products)!==Number(o.total)?`<br><span class="small">Productos: ${money(o.total_products)}</span>`:'';
  let logisticClass=logistic==='FULL'?'ship-full':logistic==='FLEX'?'ship-flex':(logistic==='A coordinar'||logistic==='Sin envío')?'ship-coord':'ship-ml';
  let needsVisualAction=saleNeedsV

function arcaNumberCaeBlock(r){let p=String(r.pto_vta||'').padStart(4,'0');let n=r.cbte_nro?String(r.cbte_nro).padStart(8,'0'):'BORRADOR';let cae=r.cae?`CAE ${esc(r.cae)}`:(String(r.status||'').toLowerCase()==='pending_to_invoice'?'Pendiente para facturar':'Sin CAE');return `<div class="arcaCbteCell"><strong>${esc(arcaTypeShort(r))}</strong><br>${esc(p+'-'+n)}<br><span class="small">${cae}</span></div>`}
function arcaStatusIcon(r){
  let st=String(r.status||'draft').toLowerCase();
  if(st==='issued'||r.cae||r.status_icon==='✅')return `<span class="arcaStatusIconCell" title="Emitida">✅</span>`;
  if(st==='draft'||st==='pending_to_invoice'||st==='pending'||r.status_icon==='📝')return `<span class="arcaStatusIconCell" title="Pendiente para facturar">📝</span>`;
  return `<span class="arcaStatusIconCell" title="Error / revisar">⚠️</span>`;
}
function arcaDoc(r){return [r.customer_doc_type||'',r.customer_doc_number||''].filter(Boolean).join(' ')||'-'}
function arcaOperation(r){return r.source_order_number||r.source_order_id||r.source_order_api_id||''}
function arcaActions(r){
  let id=encodeURIComponent(r.id||'');
  let ch=String(r.source_channel||'').toUpperCase();
  // TN debe facturarse por ID interno/API, no por número visible (#674).
  // ML puede usar pack/sale number para consolidar grupos.
  let oid=String(ch==='TN' ? (r.source_order_api_id||r.source_order_id||'') : (r.source_order_id||r.source_order_api_id||''));
  let view=id?`<button onclick="openInvoiceHtml('${esc(r.id||'')}')">Ver / imprimir PDF</button>`:'';
  let facturar=(ch&&oid&&!r.cae)?`<button onclick="issueInvoiceFromArcaReport('${esc(ch)}','${esc(oid)}')">Facturar</button>`:'';
  let borrador=(ch&&oid&&!r.cae)?`<button onclick="createInvoiceDraft('${esc(ch)}','${esc(oid)}')">Actualizar borrador</button>`:'';
  let nc=(id&&r.cae)?`<button onclick="arcaStartNoteFromInvoice('${esc(r.id||'')}','NC')">Nota de Crédito</button>`:'';
  let nd=(id&&r.cae)?`<button onclick="arcaStartNoteFromInvoice('${esc(r.id||'')}','ND')">Nota de Débito</button>`:'';
  return `<div class="arcaActionsWrap"><details class="kebabMenu"><summary title="Más acciones">⋮</summary><div class="kebabPanel">${facturar}${view}${borrador}${nc}${nd}</div></details></div>`;
}
async function issueInvoiceFromArcaReport(ch,orderId){
  await issueInvoiceFromSale(ch,orderId,{fromArcaReport:true});
}
function arcaInvoiceSearchText(r){
  let parts=[
    r.invoice_date,r.created_at,r.cbte_tipo_label,arcaTypeShort(r),r.cbte_nro,r.pto_vta,r.cae,
    r.customer_name,r.source_customer_name,r.customer_doc_type,r.customer_doc_number,r.customer_iva_condition,
    r.source_channel,r.source_user,r.source_order_id,r.source_order_number,r.source_order_api_id,r.source_pack_id,r.source_shipping_id,
    r.importe_total
  ];
  (r.lines||[]).forEach(l=>parts.push(l.sku,l.description,l.name,l.title,l.quantity,l.unit_price_gross,l.total_gross));
  return normalizar(parts.filter(v=>v!==null&&v!==undefined).join(' '));
}
function renderArcaInvoices(){
  let rows=(state.arcaRows||[]);
  let q=normalizar(qs('arcaSearch')?.value||'');
  if(q){rows=rows.filter(r=>arcaInvoiceSearchText(r).includes(q))}
  qs('arcaTable').innerHTML=`<table><thead><tr><th>Fecha</th><th>Comprobante</th><th>Cliente fiscal</th><th>Documento</th><th>IVA</th><th>Canal</th><th>Usuario</th><th>Total</th><th>Estado</th><th>⋮</th></tr></thead><tbody>${rows.map(r=>`<tr><td class="arcaDateCell">${esc(r.invoice_date||String(r.created_at||'').slice(0,10)||'')}</td><td>${arcaNumberCaeBlock(r)}</td><td><div class="arcaFiscalName">${esc(r.customer_name||r.source_customer_name||'-')}</div><span class="small">${esc(r.customer_city||'')}${r.customer_province?' · '+esc(r.customer_province):''}</span></td><td class="arcaCompactDoc">${esc(arcaDoc(r))}</td><td>${esc(r.customer_iva_condition||'-')}</td><td class="arcaChannelCell">${esc(arcaChannelLabel(r))}</td><td class="arcaUserCell">${esc(r.source_user||'')}</td><td><strong>${money(r.importe_total)}</strong></td><td>${arcaStatusIcon(r)}</td><td>${arcaActions(r)}</td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="10" class="muted" style="text-align:center">Sin comprobantes para ese filtro.</td></tr>'}</tbody></table>`;
  let total=(state.arcaRows||[]).length;
  setStatus('arcaStatus',`OK: ${rows.length}${q?' filtrados de '+total:''} comprobantes`,true)
}
async function loadArcaInvoices(){
  initArcaDates();setStatus('arcaStatus','Consultando comprobantes...');
  try{
    let lim=Number(qs('arcaLimit')?.value||100);
    let p=`/admin/arca/facturas?limit=${lim}&date_from=${encodeURIComponent(qs('arcaDesde')?.value||'')}&date_to=${encodeURIComponent(qs('arcaHasta')?.value||'')}`;
    let tipo=qs('arcaTipo')?.value||'Todos',canal=qs('arcaCanal')?.value||'Todos',concepto=qs('arcaConcepto')?.value||'Todos';
    if(tipo!=='Todos')p+=`&cbte_tipo=${encodeURIComponent(tipo)}`;
    if(canal!=='Todos')p+=`&channel=${encodeURIComponent(canal)}`;
    if(concepto!=='Todos')p+=`&concept=${encodeURIComponent(concepto)}`;
    let d=await fetchJson(p);state.arcaRows=d.items||[];renderArcaInvoices();
  }catch(e){saveLastArcaError(e,{fn:'loadArcaInvoices'});setStatus('arcaStatus','Error ARCA: '+errText(e),false);showPre('arcaOut',e)}
}

async function uploadKnowledgeBase(){
  let f=qs('knowledgeFile')?.files?.[0];
  if(!f){setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Elegí un archivo .xlsx.',false);return}
  let fd=new FormData();
  fd.append('file',f);
  try{
    setBusy(true,'Subiendo Base de Conocimiento IA','Actualizando reglas IA por SKU y lugares de retiro...');
    let r=await fetch(url('/admin/knowledge/upload'),{method:'POST',body:fd});
    let txt=await r.text();
    let d;try{d=JSON.parse(txt)}catch{d={ok:r.ok,text:txt}}
    if(!r.ok){throw d}
    let res=d.result||{};
    if(d.ok===false && !d.partial_ok && !res.partial_ok){throw d}
    let msg=`Base subida OK. Reglas: ${res.rules_upserted||0} · Lugares: ${res.pickup_locations_upserted||0} · Prompts: ${res.prompts_upserted||0}`;
    if(d.partial_ok||res.partial_ok){
      let es=res.error_summary||{};
      msg=`Base subida parcial. Reglas: ${res.rules_upserted||0} · Lugares: ${res.pickup_locations_upserted||0} · Prompts: ${res.prompts_upserted||0} · Errores: ${es.total||res.errors?.length||0}`;
    }
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus',msg,true);
    showPre('knowledgeOut',JSON.stringify(d,null,2));
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Error subiendo base: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    showPre('knowledgeOut',JSON.stringify(e,null,2));
  }finally{
    setBusy(false);
  }
}
async function showKnowledgeSetupSql(){
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson('/admin/knowledge/setup_sql');
    showPre('knowledgeOut',d.sql||JSON.stringify(d,null,2));
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','SQL de setup listo para copiar en Supabase si las tablas no existen.',true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Error obteniendo SQL: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
  }
}

function closeOpenKebabMenus(){document.querySelectorAll('details.kebabMenu[open]').forEach(d=>d.removeAttribute('open'))}
function positionOpenKebabMenus(){document.querySelectorAll('details.kebabMenu[open]').forEach(d=>{let s=d.querySelector('summary');let p=d.querySelector('.kebabPanel');if(!s||!p)return;let r=s.getBoundingClientRect();p.style.visibility='hidden';p.style.display='grid';let w=p.offsetWidth||220;let h=p.offsetHeight||180;let left=Math.min(Math.max(8,r.right-w),window.innerWidth-w-8);let top=Math.min(r.bottom+6,window.innerHeight-h-8);if(top<8)top=8;p.style.left=left+'px';p.style.top=top+'px';p.style.visibility='visible';});}
document.addEventListener('toggle',e=>{let d=e.target;if(!(d instanceof HTMLDetailsElement)||!d.classList.contains('kebabMenu'))return;if(d.open){document.querySelectorAll('details.kebabMenu[open]').forEach(x=>{if(x!==d)x.removeAttribute('open')});setTimeout(positionOpenKebabMenus,0)}},true);
window.addEventListener('scroll',positionOpenKebabMenus,true);window.addEventListener('resize',positionOpenKebabMenus);
function scrollToInventoryTool(){let box=inventoryToolBox();if(!box)return;setTimeout(()=>box.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth',block:'start'}),60)}
function toggleInventoryTool(kind){let box=inventoryToolBox();if(!box)return;closeOpenKebabMenus();box.classList.remove('hidden');if(kind==='product')renderCreateProductTool();if(kind==='bundle')showView('combos');if(kind==='link')renderLinkPublicationsTool();scrollToInventoryTool()}function invToolStatus(msg,ok=true){let el=qs('inventoryToolStatus');if(!el)return;el.textContent=msg;el.style.color=ok?'var(--ok)':'var(--bad)'}function renderCreateProductTool(){inventoryToolBox().innerHTML=`<div class="card" style="background:#fffaf0;border-color:#eee2c8"><h3>Agregar producto simple</h3><p>Alta de SKU simple. Después podés vincular publicaciones ML/TN sin asociar.</p><div class="grid"><div class="col-3"><label>SKU *</label><input id="newSku" placeholder="Ej: PC..." oninput="if(qs('linkSku'))qs('linkSku').value=this.value"></div><div class="col-5"><label>Producto *</label><input id="newName" placeholder="Nombre comercial"></div><div class="col-2"><label>Stock inicial</label><input id="newStock" type="number" step="1" value="0"></div><div class="col-2"><label>Costo</label><input id="newCost" type="number" step="0.01" placeholder="Opcional"></div></div><div class="btnrow" style="margin-top:12px"><button class="ok" onclick="createInventoryProduct()">Crear producto</button><button class="secondary" onclick="renderLinkPublicationsTool(qs('newSku')?.value||'')">Vincular publicaciones</button><button class="secondary" onclick="inventoryToolBox().classList.add('hidden')">Cerrar</button></div><div id="inventoryToolStatus" class="status"></div></div>`}
async function createInventoryProduct(){let sku=(qs('newSku').value||'').trim();let name=(qs('newName').value||'').trim();if(!sku||!name){invToolStatus('SKU y producto son obligatorios.',false);return}let body={sku,name,cost:qs('newCost').value?Number(qs('newCost').value):null,stock:Number(qs('newStock').value||0),active:true};invToolStatus('Creando producto...');try{let d=await fetchJson('/admin/v2/inventory/product',{method:'POST',body:JSON.stringify(body)});invToolStatus(`Producto creado: ${d.item?.sku||sku}`,true);qs('invSearch').value=sku;await searchInventory(0,true)}catch(e){invToolStatus('Error creando producto: '+(e?.detail?JSON.stringify(e.detail):JSON.stringify(e)),false)}}

async function uploadKnowledgeBase(){
  let f=qs('knowledgeFile')?.files?.[0];
  if(!f){setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Elegí un archivo .xlsx.',false);return}
  let fd=new FormData();
  fd.append('file',f);
  try{
    setBusy(true,'Subiendo Base de Conocimiento IA','Actualizando reglas IA por SKU y lugares de retiro...');
    let r=await fetch(url('/admin/knowledge/upload'),{method:'POST',body:fd});
    let txt=await r.text();
    let d;try{d=JSON.parse(txt)}catch{d={ok:r.ok,text:txt}}
    if(!r.ok){throw d}
    let res=d.result||{};
    if(d.ok===false && !d.partial_ok && !res.partial_ok){throw d}
    let msg=`Base subida OK. Reglas: ${res.rules_upserted||0} · Lugares: ${res.pickup_locations_upserted||0} · Prompts: ${res.prompts_upserted||0}`;
    if(d.partial_ok||res.partial_ok){
      let es=res.error_summary||{};
      msg=`Base subida parcial. Reglas: ${res.rules_upserted||0} · Lugares: ${res.pickup_locations_upserted||0} · Prompts: ${res.prompts_upserted||0} · Errores: ${es.total||res.errors?.length||0}`;
    }
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus',msg,true);
    showPre('knowledgeOut',JSON.stringify(d,null,2));
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Error subiendo base: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    showPre('knowledgeOut',JSON.stringify(e,null,2));
  }finally{
    setBusy(false);
  }
}
async function showKnowledgeSetupSql(){
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson('/admin/knowledge/setup_sql');
    showPre('knowledgeOut',d.sql||JSON.stringify(d,null,2));
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','SQL de setup listo para copiar en Supabase si las tablas no existen.',true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Error obteniendo SQL: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
  }
}

ULL/FLEX: Full queda como bodega; Flex conserva su lógica propia.
  if(logistic==='FULL'&&(blob.includes('ready_to_ship')||blob.includes('pending')||blob.includes('handling')||blob.includes('packed')))return 'Procesando en bodega';

  // Si fue refrescado desde ML y es Mercado Envíos común, evitamos falso rojo por status base ready_to_ship.
  // ML suele conservar ready_to_ship mientras el subestado/seguimiento real avanza.
  if(ch==='ML'&&logistic==='Mercado Envíos'&&refreshed&&blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'En camino';

  if(blob.includes('ready_to_ship'))return 'Listo para despachar';
  if(blob.includes('not_shipped')||blob.includes('unpacked')||blob.includes('unfulfilled'))return 'Sin despachar';
  if(blob.includes('pending'))return 'Pendiente';
  if(opt)return opt;
  return '';
}
function shippingStateClass(label){
  let raw=String(label||'').toLowerCase();
  if(raw.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered'))return 'delivered';
  if(raw.includes('a coordinar'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('pendiente'))return 'pending';
  if(raw.includes('despacharemos'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('procesando'))return 'other';
  if(raw.includes('listo')||raw.includes('despachar')||raw.includes('sin despachar'))return 'pending';
  return 'other';
}
function invoiceOrderId(o,ch){
  if(ch==='ML'){
    let ids=Array.isArray(o.child_order_ids)?o.child_order_ids.filter(Boolean):[];
    if(ids.length)return ids[0];
  }
  return o.external_order_id||o.id||'';
}
function invoiceButton(o,ch){
  // Sólo ventas entregadas y todavía no facturadas muestran la acción.
  // Sin icono significa: ya facturada o todavía no corresponde facturar.
  let st=String(o.invoice_status||o.arca_status||'').toLowerCase();
  let hasCae=!!(o.invoice_cae||o.cae||o.arca_cae);
  if(hasCae||st==='issued')return '';
  let delivered=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').trim().toLowerCase()==='entregado';
  if(!delivered)return '';
  let oid=invoiceOrderId(o,ch);
  if(!oid)return '';
  return `<div class="invoiceMiniWrap"><details class="kebabMenu invoiceKebab"><summary class="invoiceStatusIcon draft" title="Pendiente de facturación">📄⚠️</summary><div class="kebabPanel"><button onclick="issueInvoiceFromSale('${jsq(ch)}','${jsq(oid)}')">Facturar</button></div></details></div>`;
}
function isTnMotoShipping(o){
  let opt=String(o.shipping_option||o.tn_shipping_option||'').toLowerCase();
  return opt.includes('moto')||opt.includes('motomensaj')||opt.includes('mensajería')||opt.includes('mensajeria');
}
function canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch){
  if(ch!=='TN')return false;
  if(!isTnMotoShipping(o))return false;
  let st=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').toLowerCase();
  let raw=shippingStatusText(o);
  let already=!!(o.tn_manual_delivered||o.manual_delivered)||st.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered')||raw.includes('manual_delivered');
  if(already)return false;
  return st.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('shipped');
}
function tnDeliveredButton(o,ch){
  if(!canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch))return '';
  let oid=String(o.external_order_id||'');
  if(!oid)return '';
  let label=String(orderNumber(o,ch)||oid).replace(/'/g,'');
  return `<br><button class="secondary smallBtn" onclick="markTnMotoDelivered('${esc(oid)}','${esc(label)}')">Entregado</button>`;
}
async function markTnMotoDelivered(orderId,label){
  if(!confirm(`Marcar ${label||orderId} como ENTREGADO?\n\nPrimero intento reflejarlo en Tienda Nube. Si TN lo rechaza, igual queda cerrado en el ERP y se guarda el error.`))return;
  setBusy(true,'Marcando entregado','Intentando marcar entregado en Tienda Nube y cerrando ERP...');
  setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Marcando entregado...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/tn/orders/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/mark_delivered_manual?sync_tn=true`,{method:'POST'});
    let tnMsg=d.tn_api_ok?'ERP cerrado; TN respondió OK pero para moto puede quedar shipped':'ERP cerrado; TN no aceptó delivered (ver raw/debug)';
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus',`OK: ${label||orderId} marcado Entregado · ${tnMsg}`,true);
    await loadRecent('TN',state.sales.TN.offset||0);
    loadDashboard(true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Error marcando entregado: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('markTnMotoDelivered',e);
  }finally{setBusy(false)}
}

function orderCard(o,ch){
  let lines=linesForOrder(o);
  let display=lines.map(l=>`<div class="lineItem"><div><strong>${esc(l.sku)}</strong></div><div>${esc(l.name||'')}</div><div>Cant: <strong>${esc(l.quantity)}</strong></div><div>${l.unit_price!==''?money(l.unit_price):''}</div><div>${l.prev!==undefined?`Stock ${esc(l.prev)} → ${esc(l.next)}`:(l.subtotal?money(l.subtotal):'')}</div></div>`).join('')||'<div class="muted">Sin líneas visibles todavía.</div>';
  let sub=subOrderText(o,ch);
  let logistic=logisticLabel(o,ch);
  let logState=shippingStateLabel(o,ch);
  let act=saleNeedsAction(o,ch);
  let stateCls=shippingStateClass(logState);
  let stateHtml=logState?`<span class="shippingAction ${stateCls}">${esc(logState)}</span>`:'';
  let manualDeliveredHtml=tnDeliveredButton(o,ch);
  let showAction=!!(act&&String(act).trim().toLowerCase()!==String(logState||'').trim().toLowerCase());
  let actionHtml=showAction?`<span class="logisticsAction">${esc(act)}</span>`:'';
  let totalSub=o.total_products&&Number(o.total_products)!==Number(o.total)?`<br><span class="small">Productos: ${money(o.total_products)}</span>`:'';
  let logisticClass=logistic==='FULL'?'ship-full':logistic==='FLEX'?'ship-flex':(logistic==='A coordinar'||logistic==='Sin envío')?'ship-coord':'ship-ml';
  let needsVisualAction=saleNeedsVisualAction(o,ch);
  let saleDate=o.display_created_at||o.sale_at||o.ml_date_closed||o.ml_date_created||o.tn_paid_at||o.tn_

=='MANUAL'||up==='ARCA')?'MANUAL':ch}
function arcaNumberCaeBlock(r){let p=String(r.pto_vta||'').padStart(4,'0');let n=r.cbte_nro?String(r.cbte_nro).padStart(8,'0'):'BORRADOR';let cae=r.cae?`CAE ${esc(r.cae)}`:(String(r.status||'').toLowerCase()==='pending_to_invoice'?'Pendiente para facturar':'Sin CAE');return `<div class="arcaCbteCell"><strong>${esc(arcaTypeShort(r))}</strong><br>${esc(p+'-'+n)}<br><span class="small">${cae}</span></div>`}
function arcaStatusIcon(r){
  let st=String(r.status||'draft').toLowerCase();
  if(st==='issued'||r.cae||r.status_icon==='✅')return `<span class="arcaStatusIconCell" title="Emitida">✅</span>`;
  if(st==='draft'||st==='pending_to_invoice'||st==='pending'||r.status_icon==='📝')return `<span class="arcaStatusIconCell" title="Pendiente para facturar">📝</span>`;
  return `<span class="arcaStatusIconCell" title="Error / revisar">⚠️</span>`;
}
function arcaDoc(r){return [r.customer_doc_type||'',r.customer_doc_number||''].filter(Boolean).join(' ')||'-'}
function arcaOperation(r){return r.source_order_number||r.source_order_id||r.source_order_api_id||''}
function arcaActions(r){
  let id=encodeURIComponent(r.id||'');
  let ch=String(r.source_channel||'').toUpperCase();
  // TN debe facturarse por ID interno/API, no por número visible (#674).
  // ML puede usar pack/sale number para consolidar grupos.
  let oid=String(ch==='TN' ? (r.source_order_api_id||r.source_order_id||'') : (r.source_order_id||r.source_order_api_id||''));
  let view=id?`<button onclick="openInvoiceHtml('${esc(r.id||'')}')">Ver / imprimir PDF</button>`:'';
  let facturar=(ch&&oid&&!r.cae)?`<button onclick="issueInvoiceFromArcaReport('${esc(ch)}','${esc(oid)}')">Facturar</button>`:'';
  let borrador=(ch&&oid&&!r.cae)?`<button onclick="createInvoiceDraft('${esc(ch)}','${esc(oid)}')">Actualizar borrador</button>`:'';
  let nc=(id&&r.cae)?`<button onclick="arcaStartNoteFromInvoice('${esc(r.id||'')}','NC')">Nota de Crédito</button>`:'';
  let nd=(id&&r.cae)?`<button onclick="arcaStartNoteFromInvoice('${esc(r.id||'')}','ND')">Nota de Débito</button>`:'';
  return `<div class="arcaActionsWrap"><details class="kebabMenu"><summary title="Más acciones">⋮</summary><div class="kebabPanel">${facturar}${view}${borrador}${nc}${nd}</div></details></div>`;
}
async function issueInvoiceFromArcaReport(ch,orderId){
  await issueInvoiceFromSale(ch,orderId,{fromArcaReport:true});
}
function arcaInvoiceSearchText(r){
  let parts=[
    r.invoice_date,r.created_at,r.cbte_tipo_label,arcaTypeShort(r),r.cbte_nro,r.pto_vta,r.cae,
    r.customer_name,r.source_customer_name,r.customer_doc_type,r.customer_doc_number,r.customer_iva_condition,
    r.source_channel,r.source_user,r.source_order_id,r.source_order_number,r.source_order_api_id,r.source_pack_id,r.source_shipping_id,
    r.importe_total
  ];
  (r.lines||[]).forEach(l=>parts.push(l.sku,l.description,l.name,l.title,l.quantity,l.unit_price_gross,l.total_gross));
  return normalizar(parts.filter(v=>v!==null&&v!==undefined).join(' '));
}
function renderArcaInvoices(){
  let rows=(state.arcaRows||[]);
  let q=normalizar(qs('arcaSearch')?.value||'');
  if(q){rows=rows.filter(r=>arcaInvoiceSearchText(r).includes(q))}
  qs('arcaTable').innerHTML=`<table><thead><tr><th>Fecha</th><th>Comprobante</th><th>Cliente fiscal</th><th>Documento</th><th>IVA</th><th>Canal</th><th>Usuario</th><th>Total</th><th>Estado</th><th>⋮</th></tr></thead><tbody>${rows.map(r=>`<tr><td class="arcaDateCell">${esc(r.invoice_date||String(r.created_at||'').slice(0,10)||'')}</td><td>${arcaNumberCaeBlock(r)}</td><td><div class="arcaFiscalName">${esc(r.customer_name||r.source_customer_name||'-')}</div><span class="small">${esc(r.customer_city||'')}${r.customer_province?' · '+esc(r.customer_province):''}</span></td><td class="arcaCompactDoc">${esc(arcaDoc(r))}</td><td>${esc(r.customer_iva_condition||'-')}</td><td class="arcaChannelCell">${esc(arcaChannelLabel(r))}</td><td class="arcaUserCell">${esc(r.source_user||'')}</td><td><strong>${money(r.importe_total)}</strong></td><td>${arcaStatusIcon(r)}</td><td>${arcaActions(r)}</td></tr>`).join('')||'<tr><td colspan="10" class="muted" style="text-align:center">Sin comprobantes para ese filtro.</td></tr>'}</tbody></table>`;
  let total=(state.arcaRows||[]).length;
  setStatus('arcaStatus',`OK: ${rows.length}${q?' filtrados de '+total:''} comprobantes`,true)
}
async function loadArcaInvoices(){
  initArcaDates();setStatus('arcaStatus','Consultando comprobantes...');
  try{
    let lim=Number(qs('arcaLimit')?.value||100);
    let p=`/admin/arca/facturas?limit=${lim}&date_from=${encodeURIComponent(qs('arcaDesde')?.value||'')}&date_to=${encodeURIComponent(qs('arcaHasta')?.value||'')}`;
    let tipo=qs('arcaTipo')?.value||'Todos',canal=qs('arcaCanal')?.value||'Todos',concepto=qs('arcaConcepto')?.value||'Todos';
    if(tipo!=='Todos')p+=`&cbte_tipo=${encodeURIComponent(tipo)}`;
    if(canal!=='Todos')p+=`&channel=${encodeURIComponent(canal)}`;
    if(concepto!=='Todos')p+=`&concept=${encodeURIComponent(concepto)}`;
    let d=await fetchJson(p);state.arcaRows=d.items||[];renderArcaInvoices();
  }catch(e){saveLastArcaError(e,{fn:'loadArcaInvoices'});setStatus('arcaStatus','Error ARCA: '+errText(e),false);showPre('arcaOut',e)}
}

async function uploadKnowledgeBase(){
  let f=qs('knowledgeFile')?.files?.[0];
  if(!f){setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Elegí un archivo .xlsx.',false);return}
  let fd=new FormData();
  fd.append('file',f);
  try{
    setBusy(true,'Subiendo Base de Conocimiento IA','Actualizando reglas IA por SKU y lugares de retiro...');
    let r=await fetch(url('/admin/knowledge/upload'),{method:'POST',body:fd});
    let txt=await r.text();
    let d;try{d=JSON.parse(txt)}catch{d={ok:r.ok,text:txt}}
    if(!r.ok){throw d}
    let res=d.result||{};
    if(d.ok===false && !d.partial_ok && !res.partial_ok){throw d}
    let msg=`Base subida OK. Reglas: ${res.rules_upserted||0} · Lugares: ${res.pickup_locations_upserted||0} · Prompts: ${res.prompts_upserted||0}`;
    if(d.partial_ok||res.partial_ok){
      let es=res.error_summary||{};
      msg=`Base subida parcial. Reglas: ${res.rules_upserted||0} · Lugares: ${res.pickup_locations_upserted||0} · Prompts: ${res.prompts_upserted||0} · Errores: ${es.total||res.errors?.length||0}`;
    }
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus',msg,true);
    showPre('knowledgeOut',JSON.stringify(d,null,2));
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Error subiendo base: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    showPre('knowledgeOut',JSON.stringify(e,null,2));
  }finally{
    setBusy(false);
  }
}
async function showKnowledgeSetupSql(){
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson('/admin/knowledge/setup_sql');
    showPre('knowledgeOut',d.sql||JSON.stringify(d,null,2));
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','SQL de setup listo para copiar en Supabase si las tablas no existen.',true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('knowledgeStatus','Error obteniendo SQL: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
  }
}

function openInvoicePreview(ch,orderId){
  if(!orderId){alert('No encontré ID de orden para preview.');return}
  window.open(url(`/admin/arca/previews/${encodeURIComponent(ch)}/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/html`),'_blank');
}
async function createInvoiceDraft(ch,orderId){
  hideArcaMonitor();
  if(!orderId){alert('No encontré ID de orden para facturar.');return}
  if(!confirm(`Crear/actualizar borrador de factura para ${ch} ${orderId}?`))return;
  setStatus(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasStatus','Creando/actualizando borrador de factura...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/arca/orders/${encodeURIComponent(ch)}/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/draft`,{method:'POST',body:JSON.stringify({concept:'Productos'})});
    let inv=d.invoice||{};
    let msg=d.updated?'Borrador actualizado':(d.duplicate?'Ya estaba emitida':'Borrador creado');
    setStatus(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasStatus',`${msg}: ${inv.cbte_tipo_label||''} ${inv.pto_vta||''}-${inv.cbte_nro||'BORRADOR'} · ${inv.customer_name||''} · ${money(inv.importe_total)}`,true);
    loadRecent(ch,state.sales[ch]?.offset||0);
    loadArcaInvoices();

  }catch(e){setStatus(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasStatus','Error creando borrador: '+(e.message||JSON.stringify(e)),false);console.error('createInvoiceDraft',e)}
}
async function issueInvoiceFromSale(ch,orderId,opts={}){
  hideArcaMonitor();
  if(!orderId){alert('No encontré ID de orden para emitir.');return}
  let ok=confirm(`Emitir comprobante REAL en ARCA para ${ch} ${orderId}?\n\nRevisá que el preview/borrador tenga receptor fiscal e importe correctos antes de aceptar.`);
  if(!ok)return;
  setArcaAndSalesStatus(ch,'Emitiendo comprobante real en ARCA. Esperá a que termine, no vuelvas a hacer clic...',null);
  setBusy(true,'Facturando en ARCA','Emitiendo CAE, generando PDF y despachando según canal. Esto puede tardar unos segundos.');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/arca/orders/${encodeURIComponent(ch)}/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/issue`,{method:'POST',body:JSON.stringify({concept:'Productos'})});
    let inv=d.invoice||{};
    let dispatch=d.post_issue_dispatch||{};
    let ml=dispatch.ml_upload||{};
    let extra='';
    if(String(ch).toUpperCase()==='ML'){
      if(ml.ok&&ml.already_uploaded)extra=' · ML ya tenía factura';
      else if(ml.ok)extra=' · PDF subido a ML';
      else if(ml.skipped)extra=' · ML pendiente';
    }
    setArcaAndSalesStatus(ch,`Emitida OK: ${inv.cbte_letra||''} ${String(inv.pto_vta||'').padStart(4,'0')}-${String(inv.cbte_nro||'').padStart(8,'0')} · CAE ${inv.cae||''}${extra}`,true);
    await loadArcaInvoices();
    loadRecent(ch,state.sales[ch]?.offset||0);
  }catch(e){
    setArcaAndSalesStatus(ch,'Error emitiendo: '+(e.message||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('issueInvoiceFromSale',e);
  }finally{
    setBusy(false);
  }
}

  }

function arcaManualBestTnPrice(item){
  let listings=(item&&item.listings)||[];
  let tn=listings.find(l=>String(l.marketplace||'').toUpperCase()==='TN'&&Number(l.price||0)>0)||listings.find(l=>Number(l.price||0)>0);
  return tn?Number(tn.price||0):0;
}

function openInvoicePreview(ch,orderId){
  if(!orderId){alert('No encontré ID de orden para preview.');return}
  window.open(url(`/admin/arca/previews/${encodeURIComponent(ch)}/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/html`),'_blank');
}
async function createInvoiceDraft(ch,orderId){
  hideArcaMonitor();
  if(!orderId){alert('No encontré ID de orden para facturar.');return}
  if(!confirm(`Crear/actualizar borrador de factura para ${ch} ${orderId}?`))return;
  setStatus(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasStatus','Creando/actualizando borrador de factura...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/arca/orders/${encodeURIComponent(ch)}/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/draft`,{method:'POST',body:JSON.stringify({concept:'Productos'})});
    let inv=d.invoice||{};
    let msg=d.updated?'Borrador actualizado':(d.duplicate?'Ya estaba emitida':'Borrador creado');
    setStatus(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasStatus',`${msg}: ${inv.cbte_tipo_label||''} ${inv.pto_vta||''}-${inv.cbte_nro||'BORRADOR'} · ${inv.customer_name||''} · ${money(inv.importe_total)}`,true);
    loadRecent(ch,state.sales[ch]?.offset||0);
    loadArcaInvoices();

  }catch(e){setStatus(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasStatus','Error creando borrador: '+(e.message||JSON.stringify(e)),false);console.error('createInvoiceDraft',e)}
}
async function issueInvoiceFromSale(ch,orderId,opts={}){
  hideArcaMonitor();
  if(!orderId){alert('No encontré ID de orden para emitir.');return}
  let ok=confirm(`Emitir comprobante REAL en ARCA para ${ch} ${orderId}?\n\nRevisá que el preview/borrador tenga receptor fiscal e importe correctos antes de aceptar.`);
  if(!ok)return;
  setArcaAndSalesStatus(ch,'Emitiendo comprobante real en ARCA. Esperá a que termine, no vuelvas a hacer clic...',null);
  setBusy(true,'Facturando en ARCA','Emitiendo CAE, generando PDF y despachando según canal. Esto puede tardar unos segundos.');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/arca/orders/${encodeURIComponent(ch)}/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/issue`,{method:'POST',body:JSON.stringify({concept:'Productos'})});
    let inv=d.invoice||{};
    let dispatch=d.post_issue_dispatch||{};
    let ml=dispatch.ml_upload||{};
    let extra='';
    if(String(ch).toUpperCase()==='ML'){
      if(ml.ok&&ml.already_uploaded)extra=' · ML ya tenía factura';
      else if(ml.ok)extra=' · PDF subido a ML';
      else if(ml.skipped)extra=' · ML pendiente';
    }
    setArcaAndSalesStatus(ch,`Emitida OK: ${inv.cbte_letra||''} ${String(inv.pto_vta||'').padStart(4,'0')}-${String(inv.cbte_nro||'').padStart(8,'0')} · CAE ${inv.cae||''}${extra}`,true);
    await loadArcaInvoices();
    loadRecent(ch,state.sales[ch]?.offset||0);
  }catch(e){
    setArcaAndSalesStatus(ch,'Error emitiendo: '+(e.message||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('issueInvoiceFromSale',e);
  }finally{
    setBusy(false);
  }
}

let arcaManualSeq=0;
function arcaManualInit(){
  if(qs('arcaManualLines') && !qs('arcaManualLines').children.length){
    if(!qs('amCustomerName').value)qs('amCustomerName').value='Consumidor Final';
    if(!qs('amLocalidad').value)qs('amLocalidad').value='Ciudad Autónoma de Buenos Aires';
    arcaManualAddLine({sku:'',description:'',quantity:1,unit_price_gross:''});
  }
}
function arcaManualLineHtml(id,d={}){
  return `<div class="marketBox arcaLine" data-id="${id}" style="grid-template-columns:120px 1fr 85px 110px 82px 44px">
    <div><label>SKU</label><input class="amSku" value="${esc(d.sku||'')}"></div>
    <div class="fieldRel"><label>Producto / servicio</label><input class="amDesc" value="${esc(d.description||'')}" oninput="arcaManualProductSearch(this)" autocomplete="off"><div class="arcaSuggest"></div></div>
    <div><label>Cant.</label><input class="amQty" type="number" step="0.01" value="${esc(d.quantity||1)}"></div>
    <div><label>Precio final</label><input class="amUnit" type="number" step="0.01" value="${esc(d.unit_price_gross||'')}"></div>
    <div><label>IVA %</label><input class="amIva" type="number" step="0.01" value="${esc(d.iva_pct||21)}"></div>
    <div><label>&nbsp;</label><button class="secondary" onclick="this.closest('.arcaLine').remove()">×</button></div>
  </div>`;
}
function arcaManualAddLine(d={}){let box=qs('arcaManualLines');if(!box)return;arcaManualSeq++;box.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend',arcaManualLineHtml(arcaManualSeq,d))}
function arcaManualBestTnPrice(item){
  let listings=(item&&item.listings)||[];
  let tn=listings.find(l=>String(l.marketplace||'').toUpperCase()==='TN'&&Number(l.price||0)>0)||listings.find(l=>Number(l.price||0)>0);
  return tn?Number(tn.price||0):0;
}

function isTnMotoShipping(o){
  let opt=String(o.shipping_option||o.tn_shipping_option||'').toLowerCase();
  return opt.includes('moto')||opt.includes('motomensaj')||opt.includes('mensajería')||opt.includes('mensajeria');
}
function canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch){
  if(ch!=='TN')return false;
  if(!isTnMotoShipping(o))return false;
  let st=String(shippingStateLabel(o,ch)||'').toLowerCase();
  let raw=shippingStatusText(o);
  let already=!!(o.tn_manual_delivered||o.manual_delivered)||st.includes('entregado')||raw.includes('delivered')||raw.includes('manual_delivered');
  if(already)return false;
  return st.includes('en camino')||raw.includes('shipped');
}
function tnDeliveredButton(o,ch){
  if(!canMarkTnDelivered(o,ch))return '';
  let oid=String(o.external_order_id||'');
  if(!oid)return '';
  let label=String(orderNumber(o,ch)||oid).replace(/'/g,'');
  return `<br><button class="secondary smallBtn" onclick="markTnMotoDelivered('${esc(oid)}','${esc(label)}')">Entregado</button>`;
}
async function markTnMotoDelivered(orderId,label){
  if(!confirm(`Marcar ${label||orderId} como ENTREGADO?\n\nPrimero intento reflejarlo en Tienda Nube. Si TN lo rechaza, igual queda cerrado en el ERP y se guarda el error.`))return;
  setBusy(true,'Marcando entregado','Intentando marcar entregado en Tienda Nube y cerrando ERP...');
  setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Marcando entregado...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/tn/orders/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/mark_delivered_manual?sync_tn=true`,{method:'POST'});
    let tnMsg=d.tn_api_ok?'ERP cerrado; TN respondió OK pero para moto puede quedar shipped':'ERP cerrado; TN no aceptó delivered (ver raw/debug)';
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus',`OK: ${label||orderId} marcado Entregado · ${tnMsg}`,true);
    await loadRecent('TN',state.sales.TN.offset||0);
    loadDashboard(true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Error marcando entregado: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('markTnMotoDelivered',e);
  }finally{setBusy(false)}
}

function orderCard(o,ch){
  let lines=linesForOrder(o);
  let display=lines.map(l=>`<div class="lineItem"><div><strong>${esc(l.sku)}</strong></div><div>${esc(l.name||'')}</div><div>Cant: <strong>${esc(l.quantity)}</strong></div><div>${l.unit_price!==''?money(l.unit_price):''}</div><div>${l.prev!==undefined?`Stock ${esc(l.prev)} → ${esc(l.next)}`:(l.subtotal?money(l.subtotal):'')}</div></div>`).join('')||'<div class="muted">Sin líneas visibles todavía.</div>';
  let sub=subOrderText(o,ch);
  let logistic=logisticLabel(o,ch);
  let logState=shippingStateLabel(o,ch);
  let act=saleNeedsAction(o,ch);
  let stateCls=shippingStateClass(logState);
  let stateHtml=logState?`<span class="shippingAction ${stateCls}">${esc(logState)}</span>`:'';
  let manualDeliveredHtml=tnDeliveredButton(o,ch);
  let showAction=!!(act&&String(act).trim().toLowerCase()!==String(logState||'').trim().toLowerCase());
  let actionHtml=showAction?`<span class="logisticsAction">${esc(act)}</span>`:'';
  let totalSub=o.total_products&&Number(o.total_products)!==Number(o.total)?`<br><span class="small">Productos: ${money(o.total_products)}</span>`:'';
  let logisticClass=logistic==='FULL'?'ship-full':logistic==='FLEX'?'ship-flex':(logistic==='A coordinar'||logistic==='Sin envío')?'ship-coord':'ship-ml';
  let needsVisualAction=saleNeedsVisualAction(o,ch);
  let saleDate=o.display_created_at||o.sale_at||o.ml_date_closed||o.ml_date_created||o.tn_paid_at||o.tn_created_at||o.created_at;
  return `<div class="orderCard ${needsVisualAction?'actionSale':''}"><div class="orderHead"><div><strong>${esc(orderNumber(o,ch))}</strong>${sub?`<br><span class="small">${sub}</span>`:''}<br><span class="small">${dateAR(saleDate)}</span></div><div>${channelCustomerHtml(o,ch)}</div><div class="orderLogisticsBlock"><span class="pill ${logisticClass} shippingPill">${esc(logistic)}</span><br><span class="orderPayStatus">${esc(orderStatusLabel(o,ch))}</span>${stateHtml}${manualDeliveredHtml}${actionHtml}</div><div><strong>${money(o.total)}</strong>${totalSub}<br><span class="small">${countLabel(lines.length)}</span></div><div>${invoiceButton(o,ch)}</div></div><div class="orderLines">${display}</div></div>`
}


function ordersTable(items,channel){if(!items||!items.length)return '<div class="card"><p>No hay ventas capturadas.</p></div>';return items.map(o=>orderCard(o,channel)).join('')}
function salesLimit(ch){let el=qs(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasLimit');return Number(el?.value||20)}
function salesSearch(ch){let el=qs(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasSearch');return (el?.value||'').trim()}
function debouncedSales(ch){clearTimeout(timers['sales_'+ch]);timers['sales_'+ch]=setTimeout(()=>{let q=salesSearch(ch);let lc=ch.toLowerCase();if(isShortSearch(q)){if(qs(lc+'VentasTable'))qs(lc+'VentasTable').innerHTML='<div class="card"><p>'+esc(minSearchMessage())+'</p></div>';if(qs(lc+'VentasPager'))qs(lc+'VentasPager').innerHTML='';setStatus(lc+'VentasStatus',minSearchMessage(),'warn');return}loadRecent(ch,0)},350)}
function clearSalesSearch(ch){let el=qs(ch.toLowerCase()+'VentasSearch');if(el)el.value='';loadRecent(ch,0)}
function mlSalesRefreshUrl(opts={}){let limit=Number(opts.limit||50);let url='/admin/ml/orders/refresh-pending-shipping?limit='+encodeURIComponent(limit);if(opts.force)url+='&force=true';return url}
async function refreshShippingPending(ch,opts={}){let lc=String(ch||'').toLowerCase();let sid=lc+'VentasStatus';if(!['ml','tn'].includes(lc))return;let label=ch==='ML'?'Mercado Libre':'Tienda Nube';let silent=!!opts.silent;let reload=opts.reload!==false;if(!silent&&!confirm('Refrescar estados de envío no entrega

;
  setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Marcando entregado...');
  try{
    let d=await fetchJson(`/admin/tn/orders/${encodeURIComponent(orderId)}/mark_delivered_manual?sync_tn=true`,{method:'POST'});
    let tnMsg=d.tn_api_ok?'ERP cerrado; TN respondió OK pero para moto puede quedar shipped':'ERP cerrado; TN no aceptó delivered (ver raw/debug)';
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus',`OK: ${label||orderId} marcado Entregado · ${tnMsg}`,true);
    await loadRecent('TN',state.sales.TN.offset||0);
    loadDashboard(true);
  }catch(e){
    setStatus('tnVentasStatus','Error marcando entregado: '+(e.message||e.detail||JSON.stringify(e)),false);
    console.error('markTnMotoDelivered',e);
  }finally{setBusy(false)}
}

function orderCard(o,ch){
  let lines=linesForOrder(o);
  let display=lines.map(l=>`<div class="lineItem"><div><strong>${esc(l.sku)}</strong></div><div>${esc(l.name||'')}</div><div>Cant: <strong>${esc(l.quantity)}</strong></div><div>${l.unit_price!==''?money(l.unit_price):''}</div><div>${l.prev!==undefined?`Stock ${esc(l.prev)} → ${esc(l.next)}`:(l.subtotal?money(l.subtotal):'')}</div></div>`).join('')||'<div class="muted">Sin líneas visibles todavía.</div>';
  let sub=subOrderText(o,ch);
  let logistic=logisticLabel(o,ch);
  let logState=shippingStateLabel(o,ch);
  let act=saleNeedsAction(o,ch);
  let stateCls=shippingStateClass(logState);
  let stateHtml=logState?`<span class="shippingAction ${stateCls}">${esc(logState)}</span>`:'';
  let manualDeliveredHtml=tnDeliveredButton(o,ch);
  let showAction=!!(act&&String(act).trim().toLowerCase()!==String(logState||'').trim().toLowerCase());
  let actionHtml=showAction?`<span class="logisticsAction">${esc(act)}</span>`:'';
  let totalSub=o.total_products&&Number(o.total_products)!==Number(o.total)?`<br><span class="small">Productos: ${money(o.total_products)}</span>`:'';
  let logisticClass=logistic==='FULL'?'ship-full':logistic==='FLEX'?'ship-flex':(logistic==='A coordinar'||logistic==='Sin envío')?'ship-coord':'ship-ml';
  let needsVisualAction=saleNeedsVisualAction(o,ch);
  let saleDate=o.display_created_at||o.sale_at||o.ml_date_closed||o.ml_date_created||o.tn_paid_at||o.tn_created_at||o.created_at;
  return `<div class="orderCard ${needsVisualAction?'actionSale':''}"><div class="orderHead"><div><strong>${esc(orderNumber(o,ch))}</strong>${sub?`<br><span class="small">${sub}</span>`:''}<br><span class="small">${dateAR(saleDate)}</span></div><div>${channelCustomerHtml(o,ch)}</div><div class="orderLogisticsBlock"><span class="pill ${logisticClass} shippingPill">${esc(logistic)}</span><br><span class="orderPayStatus">${esc(orderStatusLabel(o,ch))}</span>${stateHtml}${manualDeliveredHtml}${actionHtml}</div><div><strong>${money(o.total)}</strong>${totalSub}<br><span class="small">${countLabel(lines.length)}</span></div><div>${invoiceButton(o,ch)}</div></div><div class="orderLines">${display}</div></div>`
}

async function refreshShippingPending(ch,opts={}){let lc=String(ch||'').toLowerCase();let sid=lc+'VentasStatus';if(!['ml','tn'].includes(lc))return;let label=ch==='ML'?'Mercado Libre':'Tienda Nube';let silent=!!opts.silent;let reload=opts.reload!==false;if(!silent&&!confirm('Refrescar estados de envío no entregados de '+label+'?\n\nSe consulta la API y se saltea sólo lo que ya figure Entregado.'))return;if(!silent)setBusy(true,'Refrescando envíos '+ch,'Consultando estados no entregados...');setStatus(sid,(silent?'Actualizando envíos ML antes de mostrar ventas...':'Refrescando estados no entregados...'));try{let path=lc==='ml'?mlSalesRefreshUrl(opts):`/admin/${lc}/orders/refresh_shipping_pending?limit=50&days=30&scan_limit=250`;let d=await fetchJson(path,{method:'POST',skipLastJson:!!silent});let errors=Number(d.errors_count??d.error_count??0);let done=Number(d.processed_count??d.refreshed_count??0);let skipped=Number(d.skipped_count??0);setStatus(sid,`Refresh ${ch}: ${done} consultadas/actualizadas, ${skipped} salteadas, ${errors} errores`,errors?false:true);if(reload)await loadRecent(ch,0,{skipShippingRefresh:true});if(!silent)loadDashboard(true);return d}catch(e){setStatus(sid,'Error refresh envíos: '+errText(e),false);console.error('refreshShippingPending',e);if(!silent)saveLastJson(e);return null}finally{if(!silent)setBusy(false)}}
function pagerHtml(ch,d){let limit=Number(d.limit||salesLimit(ch)||20),offset=Number(d.offset||0),total=Number(d.total||0);let from=total?offset+1:0;let to=Math.min(offset+(d.items||[]).length,total||offset+(d.items||[]).length);let prev=Math.max(0,offset-limit);let next=offset+limit;let prevDisabled=offset<=0?'disabled':'';let nextDisabled=!d.has_more?'disabled':'';return `<button class="secondary" ${prevDisabled} onclick="loadRecent('${ch}',${prev})">Anterior</button><span class="pill">Mostrando ${from}–${to}${total?` de ${total}`:''}</span><button class="secondary" ${nextDisabled} onclick="loadRecent('${ch}',${next})">Siguiente</button>`}
async function loadRecent(ch,offset=0,opts={}){let lc=ch.toLowerCase();let sid=lc+'VentasStatus',tid=lc+'VentasTable',pid=lc+'VentasPager';let lim=salesLimit(ch);saveViewPref('ventas_'+ch.toLowerCase(),'limit',lim);let q=salesSearch(ch);if(isShortSearch(q)){if(qs(tid))qs(tid).innerHTML='<div class="card"><p>'+esc(minSearchMessage())+'</p></div>';if(qs(pid))qs(pid).innerHTML='';setStatus(sid,minSearchMessage(),'warn');return}state.sales[ch].offset=offset;if(ch==='ML'&&opts.refreshShipping&&!opts.skipShippingRefresh){await refreshShippingPending('ML',{silent:true,reload:false,limit:50})}setStatus(sid,'Consultando ventas guarda
